Puppet Organization Builds Huludao, Japan Instigates Puppet Railway Bureau to Actively Proceed

Liaoning correspondence: The importance of Huludao, located in western Liaoning and opposite Yingkou, as well as its economic value, is well known to Chinese people. Before the incident, the Northeast authorities signed a construction contract with the Dutch Harbor Construction Company at a cost of 6.4 million US dollars and started building the island. Unexpectedly, this large-scale project was suspended shortly after construction began due to the incident. After the company personnel left one after another last autumn, it became almost a completely dead port. Recently, the Japanese believed that the island is of great importance to the development of industry and culture in western Liaoning and Rehe, and is also a training port for the Rehe Railway. Most importantly, after the port is built, it can compete with Tianjin Port. With these factors, they believe that the port must be built. Therefore, the Japanese instigated the puppet Railway Bureau to start construction, and the bureau is now actively proceeding. Furthermore, the Western Shipping Company, which operates scheduled voyages between Dalian and Huludao, is eagerly awaiting the completion of the port to facilitate its business. Therefore, as an emergency measure, starting from June 1st, they extended and repaired the completed trestle bridge and the road inside the ditch, and deployed station staff and stevedores. In addition, they also plan to build a railway from Jinzhou to Huludao. According to the person in charge of the puppet bureau, after the port is built, not only can large ships enter and exit at will, but also coastal trading sailing ships will gather. Therefore, the prosperity of the port is immeasurable, and it will undoubtedly become the distribution port of western Liaoning in the future. (Northeast News Agency)

Anqin Arrives in Jiangxi to Meet Chiang, Reports on Political and Religious Situation in Tibet, Negotiates Measures for Panchen Lama to Return to Tibet

Nanchang correspondence: Anqin Lama, Shi Qingyang, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, Chen Bingguang, member, and Luo Youren, director, and Wang Luojie, secretary, arrived in the province on the express train from Nanchang-Xunyang Road at 12:30 pm on the 4th. Cai Jingjun, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Xingying, and Wang Yi, Chief of the Public Relations Section, welcomed and took care of them at the station. After crossing the river and entering the city, An and his party stayed at the Garden Hotel. An's visit was to report to Chairman Chiang on all aspects of the political and religious customs in Tibet, and to request instructions on all measures for the Panchen Lama to return to Tibet, pacify Tibetan people, and consolidate border defenses. Chiang is scheduled to meet with them at his official residence on the morning of the 6th for lengthy consultations. According to Anqin, Tibet is located in a remote border area, and transportation is difficult, which inevitably leads to estrangement. In the past, Tibetan people often mistakenly believed that the National Government had abolished religion. However, freedom of religion is enshrined in the constitution. This time, the central government's outreach to Tibet will distribute items to temples and explain that the central government allows freedom of religion and equality for all, which is deeply appreciated by the Tibetan people. All parts of Tibet are currently peaceful. However, the Dalai Lama has passed away, and there is no leader. They have specially welcomed the Panchen Lama back to Tibet to preside. The Panchen Lama has expressed his willingness to return to Tibet in accordance with the central government's wishes. In addition to requesting instructions on all measures for the Panchen Lama to return to Tibet and eliminate conflicts in Kang and Tibet, Shi Qingyang will also report on the situation of Inner Mongolian autonomy and Mongolian-Tibetan border defenses. An and his party will return to Nanjing after meeting Chiang and completing consultations. The exact date of the Panchen Lama's arrival in Jiangxi is not yet confirmed. (5th)

Reuter's Special Business Intelligence Telegram, June 7th - Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: The gold price in London today is 137 shillings and 1.5 pence, down 9 pence from yesterday.

London Silver: In the London silver market, the spot price today is 19.75 pence, down 0.0625, and the futures price is also 19.75 pence, down 0.125. There was little trading this morning, with India and the United States buying and China selling.

New York Silver: The New York silver market opened quietly, with mixed sentiments, awaiting the final developments in the silver legislation debate. The opening price for forward contracts was down 3 to 7 pounds sterling from yesterday's closing price.

Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market closed stable today. The spot price was down 4 annas, at 55 rupees and 2 annas. Futures prices were also down 4 annas.

London Special Report: In today's (7th) London gold and silver market, the transaction value of gold exceeded one million pounds sterling. The price was 137 shillings and 1.5 pence, and the US dollar exchange rate was 5.0675 yuan. This gold was apparently purchased by the United States with the Exchange Stabilization Fund in order to curb the sharp rise of the US dollar. After this large gold transaction, many US dollars were sold, so the price of the British pound against the franc and the US dollar also improved, and the French-American exchange rate also fell below the cash export point. Therefore, the trend of gold flowing from Paris to the United States may be temporarily stopped. Today's sale of gold was due to a special commission from a certain party, but it is difficult to ascertain which country the certain party belongs to. According to a certain broker, this is German gold bullion. This statement is close to the truth, because between May 31st and June 4th, Germany shipped out approximately one million pounds sterling worth of gold.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market today, the British pound exchange rate has improved because the United States purchased a large amount of gold and sold US dollars with the Exchange Stabilization Fund. The opening price of the British pound against the US dollar was 5.07 yuan, up 0.0125 from yesterday's closing price. The price fluctuated slightly in the morning, and the price at 3:00 PM was still 5.07 yuan, the same as the opening price. American-French: The opening price of the New York exchange rate for the French franc against the US dollar was 6.6075, down 1 pound sterling from yesterday.

福州 Drought Demon Causes Disaster: Fields and Soils Crack, Streams and Gullies Dry Up, Farmers Run Out of Food, Rice Prices Soar

Fuzhou Correspondence: The northwestern regions of Fujian Province experienced a drought between last autumn and summer, resulting in the complete failure of the late rice crop and widespread famine. Farmers resorted to eating wild grass and duckweed to stave off hunger, and many starved to death. Although the government transported seafood to provide relief, it was to no avail. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of spring this year, and up to April, there have been fewer than ten days of rainfall, and the drought has returned. The early rice crop planted by farmers in the higher-lying fields has withered and died due to lack of irrigation for two months. The lower-lying fields were still able to draw water from streams and gullies for cultivation, but disputes over water often arose between villages, and the district office was busy mediating. Farmers, fearing that their water would be stolen, took turns guarding their fields day and night, enduring great hardship. However, a month ago, the streams and gullies also dried up, and the crops in the lower-lying fields withered and died completely, resulting in a complete failure of the early rice crop. Recently, the scorching sun has been in the sky, with no trace of clouds. The soil has cracked due to the sun, and horses can gallop through the fields. Even the crops and vegetable leaves that are byproducts of farming are withered and useless. The livelihoods of farmers have been completely cut off. Rice prices have soared, rising from eight yuan per unit to over nine yuan in just ten days. Several farmers in the northwestern villages have committed suicide due to lack of food. It is expected that the famine will be even more severe in the next two to three months than it was last year. The village offices held a meeting last week to discuss relief measures, believing that the frequent droughts were due in part to the lack of rainfall and in part to the blockage of waterways, which prevented water from flowing. It was decided to establish a dredging committee for the northwestern villages to dredge all the blocked waterways, allowing the flow of the Min River to reach the interior. The project will be assigned to landowners on both sides of the waterways, but the project is vast and cannot be completed in less than six months, which is too slow to provide immediate relief. Some village elders announced to the villagers, starting on May 30th, that everyone should be vegetarian for three days. On June 1st, hundreds of people gathered outside the North Gate of Zhanban Village, dressed in white, wearing straw sandals, and carrying withered rice stalks and dry soil, along with a Taoist priest. They loudly beat drums and chanted loudly along the way to the Xiyuan Temple at the Fourteen Gate Bridge outside the West Gate, to invite the Three Sage Rulers to set up an altar at Lianhua Peak outside the North Gate to pray for rain. Unexpectedly, after burning incense and throwing divination blocks more than a hundred times, they were not granted permission to leave the temple to pray for rain. The hundreds of foolish farmers looked at each other in dismay and had to return dejectedly. Superstitious people therefore spread rumors that even the Three Sage Rulers could not pray for rain, and that there would be a severe drought this year with no salvation. People's hearts became increasingly uneasy. Amidst this famine panic, not only did the government have no relief measures, but the finance department, in urgent need of funds as the abandoned lunar calendar's Dragon Boat Festival was approaching, ordered the tax collectors of the villages in Minhou County to collect three million yuan of grain loans for use within two weeks. The tax deed bureau also sent police to the villages to force people to pay taxes on their deeds, and those who had already paid were required to submit their deeds for inspection, causing great disturbance. The farmers cried out in pain. (2nd)

You Guocai Denies Rumors: Sends Representative to Guangdong to Express Attitude, Cables Wang Jialie Affirming Maintenance of Peace

Guangzhou Correspondence: There have been many rumors in Guizhou Province recently. There is no question that Wang Jialie supports the Southwest. As for You Guocai, who has always been anti-Wang, it has been rumored that he is colluding with Yunnan to contain Wang. However, You recently refuted this rumor, and specially sent his chief of staff, Cai Zizheng, as a representative to Guangdong to express everything and to conduct liaison. Cai arrived in Guangzhou on the 1st and immediately visited Chen Jitang to report in detail on the current situation in Guizhou Province and You's peaceful attitude. That afternoon, he also visited Li Zongren to discuss the recent situation in Guizhou and Guangxi. On the 2nd, he went to Hong Kong to visit Hu Hanmin and made some representations. As for the rumors that You was colluding with Yunnan to covet Guizhou, You had already cabled Wang Jialie to explain the truth. "Your telegram has been received. It is my secret hope that the realization of peace here is not just empty talk. Therefore, I have been hoping for the arrival of Yin Xian for some time, but he has not been seen, which has led outsiders to speculate and spread rumors. In reality, the various departments on the west road are at peace. The rotation of defenses between Pu'an and Anlong has been misinterpreted by outsiders, and they have added to the suspicion. I informed Chief He of the situation in advance. As for the so-called troops stationed on the riverside and the Yunnan army stationed in Pan County, the Liu Brigade is still in Pan County, and Wan's own troops are still in Kunming. The main force is also in Qujing, Pingyi and other counties, and has not moved from its original defense. These are the facts and cannot be concealed. I urge you not to be misled and to order Yin Xian to set out as soon as possible according to the original plan, so as to quell the rumors. If you delay any further, there will be more troubles. I respectfully reply. You Guocai." It is also heard that You's representative, Cai Zizheng, will return to Guizhou to report after visiting Hu in Hong Kong in about a week. (2nd)

Guangxi Finance Director Arrives in Guangdong: Negotiates Economic Assistance, Promotes Sale of Guangdong Salt and Sugar, Discusses Transit Tax Rates

Guangzhou Correspondence: Due to environmental factors, the southwestern provinces need to unite to resist foreign insults. Therefore, envoys from various provinces have been traveling back and forth very frequently recently. Huang Zhongyue, the Finance Director of Guangxi Province, came to Guangdong in person on the 31st of last month to discuss various issues with the local authorities, in order to promote economic cooperation between the two provinces of Guangxi and Guangdong. According to Huang, Guangxi Province's finances have always been based on balancing income and expenditure. The annual income of national taxes in Guangxi Province is more than 13 million yuan, and the provincial taxes are more than 17 million yuan. Although the financial situation is difficult, it is still able to meet the expenses of military and political affairs. Guangxi Bank recently experienced a disturbance, and the value of banknotes fell to 7%, that is, 7 yuan per 100 yuan. It has now returned to its original state. The purpose of this trip to Guangdong is to investigate Guangdong Province's finances and to negotiate assistance in promoting the sale of Guangdong's salt and sugar products. Recently, Guangdong's salt and sugar production has been excessive, and it is planned to sell them to Yunnan and Guizhou. However, if Guangdong's salt and sugar are transported to Guizhou and Yunnan, they must pass through Guangxi Province. In the future, the tax rates for goods in transit and the measures for Guangxi Province to protect Guangdong goods in transit must be discussed in detail with the Guangdong authorities. In addition, the Xijiang River is an important transportation route between Guangdong and Guangxi, and there have been many long-standing problems with factory taxes. It is planned to take this opportunity to discuss cleaning up the problems with the Guangdong authorities. Qu Fangpu, the Finance Director of Guangdong, has been discussing with Huang in detail for several days, and various matters have been resolved one by one. Huang is scheduled to return to Guangxi on the 3rd. (2nd)

Sichuan Border Tusi Representatives Visit Deng Xihou: Deng Xihou Stages Military Demonstration, Representatives Prostrate and Kowtow

Chengdu Correspondence: Jun Zhaxi, the Tusi of Moxi in the grassland area on the border of Sichuan and Gansu, Jia Ge, the representative of Alu, the local official of Shangliuzhai, along with his entourage Suolang, Zewang, Langge, and Langba, the representative of Renqin, the Grand Tusi of the Forty-Eight Villages of Maoniugou in Songpan, have successively arrived in the province to visit Deng Xihou, the commander of the 28th Army. Deng summoned them at the army headquarters on Huaxing Street at 10:00 AM on May 26th. At that time, from the main gate of the army headquarters straight to the army commander's reception hall, the posts were densely guarded and the security was strict. The officials of the various departments were all in full uniform. Under the pomegranate tree on the left side of the reception hall was a military band. Banners and red flags were hung in front of the hall, and colorful tents were set up. A large public table was set in the center, with a very large tin pen holder, inkstone, stationery tube, and seal box on it. Deng sat in the middle in military uniform with a commander's saber hanging on his side. Deng Chongde, the director of the colonization office, stood on the right. Wen Tao, the director of the adjutant's office, Liu Xiong, the adjutant-general, and the staff members stood on the left and right. Below the steps, teams of machine gunners and infantry guarded the area in layers. Then, Jia Ge and Suolang were led in by the adjutant's office. (Zewang and Langge had returned due to illness.) Jia Ge, with a plaster on the left side of his face, dressed in Yi ethnic clothing, and Suolang walked forward with their heads bowed and prostrated themselves in front of the steps. Qi Yunbang (from Songpan), the consultant of the army headquarters, translated. Jia Ge knelt on his right knee and stated in the Yi language that Huang Zhengqing and his son of the Labrang Monastery had invaded Aba. Huang had now applied to the Gansu Provincial Government to report to Commander-in-Chief Jiang, preparing to send a large army to Aba to attack in March of this year, and also stated that the murderer who killed the local official of Shangliuzhai was a lama named Saikang, who had also fled to the Labrang Monastery. He requested the army commander to take charge, recover Aba, and not be governed by another province, and complained that he had been in the province for a long time, and the lodging was a heavy burden, and asked the army commander to give him travel expenses and send a car to Guanxian, and to issue a passport. Deng comforted them and said: (1) The border dispute between Sichuan and Gansu and the disturbance caused by Huang Zhengqing and his son have been reported to the central government by this army commander, and will be resolved after hearing from them. (2) The title given to Yang Jun Zhaxi by the former Han army commander is no longer applicable. This army commander has now appointed Yang Jun Zhaxi as the first route guerrilla commander of the Sichuan Songli Maomao Wun Colonization Supervisory Office to deter the Black Moxi area. (3) Permission is granted to purchase 15 rifles and 5,000 rounds of ammunition. (4) Immediately telegraph the Gansu Provincial Government and ask them to order the surrender of Lama Saikang for punishment according to law. (5) Tell Yang Jun Zhaxi not to make trouble. If troops from other provinces invade, he can immediately report it, and I will decide to protect him. (6) The area under the jurisdiction of the guerrilla commander should be limited to the Moxi Tusi area without orders from the army headquarters or the colonization office. At this point, Jia Ge also Chen Eluo Fanba Lao Mincheng Jia, the local official Shen Xi Tuo, requested the army commander to issue a notice prohibiting Ma Qi's officers and soldiers from invading the Sichuan border in the Eluo Hajun area. Chairman Xi Anma has telegraphed that the Gansu and Qinghai troops will never invade the Sichuan border, and hopes that people will live in peace, graze, and trade without being disturbed. Every time Deng spoke, Jia Ge and others would kowtow to show their obedience. Then Deng presented Yang Jun Zhaxi with an official seal and a triangular yellow silk flag with the words "Yang, the First Route Guerrilla Commander of the Sichuan Songli Maomao Wun Colonization Supervisory Office." The official seal and the wooden box were placed in front of Jia Ge and others, who prostrated themselves on the blanket. Jia Ge and others stood up, knelt down, and received them. Deng then took out a knife from his side and said, "I also wear a knife. My knife is to protect good people and kill bad people. Now I will also give Yang Zhaxi a knife, and tell him to protect good people and kill bad people." After Deng finished speaking, he gave awards (1) Award Yang Jun Zhaxi two pieces each of high-quality satin domestic cloth robes, a leather briefcase, a pair of leather boots, a pair of leather leggings, a felt hat, and a knife belt. (2) Award Eluo Fanba one piece each of high-quality satin domestic cloth robes and a pair of leather shoes and a felt hat. (3) Award Representative Jia Ge one piece of second-class satin robe material, a doctoral hat, and forty silver dollars. (4) Award Suolang Zewang Langge one piece of blue Haki cloth each, and ten silver dollars. Jia and others bowed and thanked them one by one, and said that they had heard the army commander's instructions clearly. "We are very ashamed that we did not offer the army commander anything of value, but we received the army commander's generous gifts. However, Commander Yang said that the army commander is our master, and it is right for a son to receive something from his mother and father. When the army commander's official documents arrive in Moxi, there will always be one or two thousand cavalrymen to greet them. Receiving the official documents is like receiving the army commander. The barbarians were originally the same kind of people, only the language is different. This is not only dead, but also on the way. Now, on behalf of Commander Yang, I thank you for your commission (kowtow) and feel like seeing the Lord of Life, like seeing the Bodhisattva." Then they said goodbye, and the music played.

After Jia Ge and others retreated, Langba, the representative of Renqin of Maoniugou, was summoned to meet. Lang was wearing a blue student uniform, with a fountain pen and a diary hanging on his left chest, yellow pants, and leather shoes, a young Werther among the Yi people. He went up the steps, prostrated himself, and knelt down, and Qi Yunbang translated. But Deng thought that Lang could speak Chinese, so he ordered him to state directly. Lang said that he had met Commander-in-Chief last spring, and the Bihe War followed. Traffic was blocked, and he did not return to Maoniugou to report to the Tusi Renqin until October. The forty-eight village Tusi were in awe of the army commander's kindness and power, and sent me to meet the army commander again. Then he presented a fine horse to thank you for the items bestowed last year. Lang also reported on the harassment and looting by Cha Nuo Ma, and planned to ask to purchase weapons for defense, and hoped to add a commission. Deng Yu said that the affairs of Sichuan have gradually improved, and the borderlands will naturally be better. I always hope that you will improve your lives, and I hope that the people of the borderlands will come to the interior to observe. After arriving in Maozhou, I will send someone to protect you out, and I will also send someone to protect you back. It is not right for Cha Nuo Ma to rob you and you to retaliate. Your Tusi in that valley are not good, and I have someone investigating. You go back and tell the Tusi to be good. I will help whoever is good. Colonizing the borderlands is to liberate you. To live in the borderlands, you must be in the interior. Now I will approve your request to purchase 12 guns. I have a whole plan for the commission, and I will give the commission after they come to see me. Then he gave awards (1) Award the Tusi Renqin one piece each of high-quality satin domestic cloth robes, a pair of leather shoes, and a felt hat. (2) Award Langba one piece of second-class satin robe material and ten silver dollars. Langba bowed his head and thanked him and retreated.

Songjiang: County Administrative Conference Opens

As the 23rd year is about to begin, all local administrative facilities, construction plans, and economic revenues and expenditures depend on the collection of local people to discuss and implement them together. Therefore, after submitting it to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval, the 9th Administrative Conference was convened on the 7th, and leaders of various agencies and chiefs of various districts were hired to attend on time. As the meeting was held as usual, Sun Shiheng and Li Chang, two members of the county party department, and Wang Zhewu, a representative of the members, delivered speeches. The conference continued in the afternoon to discuss nine cases, which were divided into groups for review and deliberation.

Niu Yongjian, Vice President of the Examination Yuan, came to Songjiang from Maqiao at about 10:00 AM yesterday. Qingpu: The Qingpu-Shanghai Road is About to Open to Traffic

The third phase of the Qingpu-Shanghai County Road project is about to be completed. Ye Yangwu and others from the county have initiated the organization of the Qingpu-Shanghai Long-Distance Bus Company. The first meeting of all the initiators was held the other day, and the company's articles of association and the procedures to be prepared for registration were discussed in detail. The planning has now been completed, and the written documents will be submitted to the county and then to the province for registration, and the road will be opened to traffic on schedule.

Wuxi: County Funds are Unified for Collection and Expenditure by the Treasury

The county government has received instructions from the Provincial Finance Department. Starting from the 23rd year, all county local tax revenues, except for the Qingzhang Fee, which is directly submitted to the provincial treasury by the county, must be deposited into the county treasury. County Magistrate Yan, upon receiving the order, specially convened the directors of the Public Security, Construction, and Education Bureaus, as well as the director of the County and City Funds Management Office, and the presidents of the Jiangsu and Farmers Banks, to discuss the matter at a meeting yesterday. The results decided to be reported to the Department for explanation and to propose the following modifications: (1) There is no doubt about the Payment Act, but according to the provincial government's order to guarantee the independence of education funding, the education item in the general reserve fee will still have a clear distinction. Also, although there are regulations in the construction project budget, the project must be designed according to actual needs and submitted for approval when the project is implemented, which is equivalent to temporary expenditure. In the future, whether the temporary expenditure of the Education and Construction Departments should follow the case of the competent department without approval, it is proposed to explain it, so that there is something to follow. (2) County funds are collected and disbursed by the treasury. There are deposits in prosperous months, and no interest is calculated. If there is a shortage in lean months, the treasury should advance funds within the total budget limit, and no interest should be calculated. (3) The purpose of the education fee accumulation fund, the kinship pension fund, and the famine prevention grain storage fund in this county has always been to deposit funds to generate interest. The income of the accumulation fund has already been included in the budget. If it is handed over to the treasury and no interest is given, it will affect the budget, and other obstacles will also occur. It is proposed to exempt it from being handed over to the treasury. (4) In accordance with the provincial treasury and Qingzhang special fund methods, a working capital of 10,000 yuan should be reserved to meet the temporary needs of various agencies and emergencies. It can be discussed and a payment order can be issued first, and then reported for approval. (5) Education funds are paid monthly, and the police team is paid in three ten-day periods. In the future, payments will be made in two installments.

Order to Form a County Construction Discussion Committee

The County Construction Discussion Committee was urged by County Magistrate Yan to organize it in accordance with the regulations. After selecting the number of committee members, they were sent to the Construction Department for approval. Now, upon receiving the Construction Department's approval, Yang Hanxi, Rong Desheng, Cai Jian San, and Gu Shuzhi have been appointed as members of the Wuxi Construction Discussion Committee, and the county will send a letter to hire them and quickly organize the committee.

A Few Cocoon Merchants Stop Weighing

Yesterday was the fourth day of the opening of the cocoon merchants. The goods from all over the city and countryside have passed their peak and are about to end. The unified cocoon price is still around 35 yuan. However, Yongtai Chang in Shitang Town, Gonghe in Bashiqiao, and Huimin and other cocoon merchants in the southern townships have stopped weighing yesterday due to the weak arrival of goods. The remaining merchants are still collecting cocoons. Merchants with a lot of goods receive 200 dans of cocoons every day, and the least receive 30 dans. In addition, the cocoon posts received by the various cocoon merchants were sent by the merchants to the Cocoon Industry Association, totaling 384 papers. Yesterday, the association forwarded them to the county government for inspection and registration. Some merchants have not yet sent the cocoon posts, and please extend the deadline for them.

Implementation of Merging Autonomous Regions

The autonomous regions of this county are divided into 17 cities and townships, and the names have been changed to district offices. In fact, they are no different from the previous city and township administrative bureaus. Therefore, for several years, due to limited funds, there have been no achievements. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, in view of this, decided to merge the autonomous regions of various counties, with a maximum of no more than 12 districts. Area, population, and economy are the criteria for dividing the districts. The county government of this county has convened several meetings with the heads of various districts and relevant parties and decided to merge them into ten districts. The candidates for district heads have also been submitted to the province for approval by the county government and will be announced in a few days.

Jiangyin: Implementation of the Fortified Zone Law

The Jiangyin Fortress Area has been ordered by the General Staff Headquarters to implement the Fortified Zone Law within a limited time to strengthen the national defense of important fortresses. After receiving the order, Commander Xie immediately implemented it according to the width of the fortress area, starting from Zhigang on the south bank of the Yangtze River and returning to Zhigang on the south bank of the Yangtze River, forming a large circle. Both the land and water within the circle are within the scope of the restricted area of the fortress area. Intermittent land and water patrol teams are dispatched to patrol the line every day, prohibiting the free entry and exit of residents on land and fishermen on the water. Ferries and boats passing through are not subject to this restriction.

Wife Killed with Knife and Husband Commits Suicide by Poisoning

Zhao Zhi, a native of Yancheng, runs a noodle shop at the entrance of the Pinxiang Teahouse in Beiwai Zhangjie Alley. He has a partner, Yao Dingjin, 27 years old, who is Zhao's brother-in-law. He married Chen Fuhai's daughter Erbao, 17 years old, from the same hometown. Her mother works in the Lixin Silk Factory in Tongyun Bridge, Wuxi. Dingjin and his wife were married last year and often had quarrels. Yesterday (the 6th) morning, the couple had another quarrel. Her husband then used a noodle-cutting knife to slash his wife's head twice, damaging the top of her skull. She has no hope of survival. Dingjin then took sulfur and saltpeter to commit suicide. Afterwards, Erbao was sent to the Gospel Hospital for treatment, and Dingjin was sent to the Zhonghe Hospital for resuscitation. He was then sent to the Public Security First Branch for interrogation.

Luo Yajie, the captain of the county police team, has been dismissed by order of the Provincial Security Department. Wu Xiaotang has been appointed to fill the vacancy. Captain Wu arrived in Danyang yesterday, visited the county magistrate, and is scheduled to take office today.

Changzhou: Completion of the Wujin Section of the Zhencheng Road

The Wujin section of the Zhencheng Road is 48 kilometers long, passing through the territories of the 1st, 15th, 16th, 17th, and 19th districts. County Magistrate Cai has been urging his subordinates to rush the construction. The projects in the 1st and 16th districts were completed at the end of May, and the project in the 17th district was also completed on the 5th of this month. The projects in the 15th and 19th districts are expected to be completed in two or three days.

Zhenjiang: Court Burns Years of Accumulated Soil

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the local court of this port burned 688 cases of opium soil handled from January to the end of December of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, and 17 opium cases that had not been resolved in the five years of the 17th, 18th, 19th, 20th and 22nd years of the Republic of China. Confiscated drugs and opium smoking utensils were burned as usual. The court also sent letters to various party and government agencies and news media to visit, with about 20 people arriving. Zhong Zihan, the president of the court, and Huang Yongzhong, the chief prosecutor, accompanied by prosecutors and clerks, supervised in front of the court gate. All the confiscated drugs were carried out of the court by coolies, and the numbers were checked in public. After being checked, the judicial police chief directed all the bailiffs to put the drugs on the kindling. For a time, the flames soared, and the burning did not end until 12:00 PM.

Haimen: Crackdown on Drug Syndicate

The Central Pharmacy of the County and City is a well-known drug trafficking syndicate in this county, selling drugs to Haimen and Qidong counties in large quantities. The other day (the 4th), Shen Fengjie and Wan Shaozhou secretly reported it to the Nantong District Supervisory Commissioner's Office. The office sent Li Guodong, a member of the Second Section, along with the informants Shen Fengjie, Wan Shaozhou, and two plainclothes police officers, to Haimen to conduct a secret investigation in the county and city. After learning the truth, they went to the county government at 2:00 PM yesterday (the 5th) to meet with County Magistrate Zhang and asked him to send the police to assist in the search. County Magistrate Zhang instructed Zhang, the captain of the Independent Squad of the Police Team, to lead ten police officers and go to the pharmacy with Li and others to search. As a result, two large wooden barrels and four foreign iron boxes of raw materials for red pills were found. The shop owner, Pu Zhuping, was arrested. That night, Section Member Li took him to the Nantong Commissioner's Office for interrogation.

Nantong: Guerrilla Team Suppresses Bandits in Fengli

Recently, large groups of sea bandits have invaded the coastal area of Jiangbei, and the losses in the Lu Ju area have been the greatest. The Jiangsu Provincial Security Department has specially transferred the maritime guerrilla team to suppress the bandits. Captain Shen Fengshan led the team south from the Haikou of Yancheng. He is currently in a firefight with the bandits in the Fengli waters. More than ten bandit ships are drifting in the ocean, and the north-south Kan Changsha Port is under temporary martial law.

Hangzhou: Child Run Over and Killed by Car on the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway

Yesterday (the 6th) at 8:00 AM, on the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway near Shangbai Town in Wukang, an American named Smith was driving a small bus from Beijing to Hangzhou. As he was driving past the area, he ran over and killed an eight-year-old child of unknown name. The road bureau detained the accident vehicle and sent it to the Wukang County Government. According to the driver Smith, who is an American, there were four passengers, one of whom was a staff member of the Laihe Foreign Company, and the other three were friends of the staff member, who came to Hangzhou from Beijing for sightseeing. On the way back to Beijing, this tragedy occurred, and they did not have passports. They were escorted to the province in the afternoon and sent to Shanghai that night to be handed over to the American Consulate in Shanghai for handling according to law.

Ningbo: Pirates on Mount Putuo's Foding Mountain Rob Three Families in a Row

On Mount Putuo's Foding Mountain, which belongs to Dinghai County, eight pirates speaking Taiwanese dialect suddenly arrived at midnight the other day. They sailed in a sailboat with double corners and twelve corners, and beat Zhang and his wife. They then went to the home of Zhu Fulai in Yan Hu Tuo Deng, hundreds of steps away from Xiaoshui Lang, and robbed him of 50 silver dollars and six pieces of clothing. Finally, they went to Xia Fuxiu's home in Xinchang and robbed him of two cotton quilts, one dou of white rice, and two bowls of vegetables. After the robbery, they left on the original boat.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Cables Executive Yuan Urging Swift Abolition of Exorbitant Taxes; Should Provinces Delay, Order Strict Enforcement

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday cabled the Executive Yuan, stating: "To the esteemed Nanjing Executive Yuan, the resolutions of the National Financial Conference regarding the permanent prohibition of additional surcharges on land taxes and the swift abolition of exorbitant taxes have been met with widespread joy, hailed as a panacea for the revival of the national economy. However, there are concerns that provincial accounting officials may use the excuse of a lack of compensatory measures to delay implementation, making it difficult for actual benefits to reach the people. It is requested that the Yuan clarify that this conference has already decided to allocate the stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol license tax, which belong to the central government, to the provinces, and to transfer judicial expenses to the national budget. This will alleviate the financial burden on the provinces and provide compensatory measures. The central government's consideration for the local governments is already comprehensive and considerate, and it is not imposing impossible demands. The two resolutions must be strictly enforced in order to uphold the authority of the nation and fulfill the hopes of the people. Your prompt attention is greatly anticipated." The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce respectfully presents this.

Li Liejun Talks About Impressions of Tour in Shandong; Shandong Officials Frugal and Hardworking; Li Plans to Go to Lushan for Rest

Mr. Li Liejun, member of the Central Committee, went to Qingdao from Shanghai last month to recuperate. He met Feng Yuxiang in Weixian and then toured various counties in Jiaodong and famous scenic spots together. After sending Feng back to Mount Tai, Li returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday (the 6th). Reporters from various newspapers visited Li at his private residence on Avenue Massenet yesterday to discuss his impressions of his tour in Shandong. Li said that his blood pressure had risen again recently and that he would go to Lushan for rest. The details of what he said are recorded below.

Abundant Products in Counties of Jiaodong

This trip to Qingdao was originally for recuperation. Since Mr. Feng came to Weixian, I toured various counties in Jiaodong and famous scenic spots with him. Because the country is in danger, I wanted to study the malpractices of China with Mr. Huanzhang and work with righteous gentlemen in the country to save it. Everywhere we went, the people were simple and honest, and the products were abundant. Most people were engaged in agriculture and commerce, so there were few vagrants. Jiaodong is therefore in a state of wealth. Most counties have county-run middle schools, and elementary schools are everywhere. Transportation, education, and industry are relatively developed. Although most customs have not been reformed, it is also a country with potential. From the chairman of the provincial government to the county magistrates, they are frugal and hardworking, which is the best among all the provinces. Unfortunately, in the trials of bandits, there is suspicion of misuse of power and interference in the judiciary. The number of people executed in various counties is alarming, so the people also say that the government of Shandong is as fierce as a tiger. If this can be improved, it will be a good government.

Mr. Feng Huanzhang's Demeanor As Before

Mr. Feng's demeanor, spirit, and perseverance are as before, but his knowledge has surpassed that of the past. He is extremely worried about the current state of the country. He believes that Japan is the most harmful foreign power to China, so he advocates actively resisting Japan and saving the country. Everywhere he went, he was warmly welcomed by the people. His speeches were also very effective in arousing public attention. Since Qingdao was taken over, the situation has been extremely complicated, and foreigners' strength is superior to that of the Chinese, as everyone knows. Fortunately, since Mayor Shen Honglie took office, he has been frugal and fair, and has earnestly reorganized the city. He has handled relations with foreigners appropriately, so there is no rampant situation. He has also vigorously supported autonomy and penetrated into the people. Therefore, Qingdao is tidy and clean on the surface, and transportation, education, and industry are developing in practice. The district offices established by the municipal government and the credit and consumer cooperatives have all achieved great results, and a group of service personnel are very energetic.

High Blood Pressure Requiring Rest in Jiangxi

The Jiaoji Railway has a debt of 40 million, with 7 million in cash and a lot of old materials. I heard that it has been proposed to build a branch line from Zhangdian via Boshan to Dakou. If this road is opened, the revenue will be doubled. Li said at the end, "My blood pressure has risen again, and I will go to Lushan for rest. I cannot talk too much. Our country is in a very dangerous period, and people across the country should rise up to save it."

American Aviator Russell Arrives in Shanghai; Says Future of Aviation in China is Promising

The Continental Daily News reports that Russell, an engineer of the Sperry Gyroscope Company of the United States, is skilled in aircraft piloting. He recently came to China at the invitation of Mr. Bolley of the Continental Aviation Company and the representative of the Sperry Company in China. He arrived in Shanghai a week ago. Mr. Russell is quite surprised by the development of commercial and military aviation in China, and says that China has a vast territory, and the future of this development is limitless. No country in the world can match it. In the future, when the government is stable, private flying will also be popular. Russell also commented on aviation routes, saying that many people say that air travel in China is too expensive, but in the future, after the promotion of commercial aviation, fares will inevitably decrease. The situation in the United States in the past was the same as in China. Later, new equipment was installed, and maintenance costs were greatly reduced, and air travel fares fell. Today, more and more people are flying, and although the fares are low, the profits are still high. China will also be like this in the future. Russell also mentioned the development of "blind flying", saying that after spending millions of US dollars researching for several years, the method of robot-piloted aircraft finally succeeded four years ago. This move has been trialed since 1913 and has now become a reality. For example, if you want to fly from Shanghai to Beiping now, you only need to install the aircraft properly and then let it depart, and five hours later, the aircraft will be in the sky over Beiping. Russell also described in detail the operation of this complex machine, which is enough to amaze those who hear it. Russell is a world traveler, and he has flown over almost every aviation route in the world. He is scheduled to go to Hangzhou before Sunday, stay for a few weeks, and then plans to go to South China, and will go to Manila, Bangkok, Saigon, Turkey, Persia, Damascus, the Netherlands, Germany, France, England, and other countries. Many aviation routes in the world rely on his planning to make them safer and more efficient.

Panchen Lama Visits National Exhibition Yesterday; Over Two Thousand Representatives From All Walks of Life Attend; Lama Delivers Earnest Speech on National Goods

In order to promote Sino-Tibetan friendship and production and sales cooperation, the National Goods Exhibition of the Penglai City Market specially invited the Panchen Lama to visit at 2 p.m. yesterday. After the exhibition was approved to be visited by the Lama, it was actively set up overnight. Inside the venue, each manufacturer used yellow silk cloth to surround the area. The front of the auditorium was covered with yellow cloth, with incense burners placed on both sides, and incense coils were hung. Attendees

Conference Staff

Presidium: Wang Yansong, Chen Binghui, Kuang Zhongmou, Liu Zhongying, Zhang Yichen; Master of Ceremonies: Leng Bingnan; Recorder: Zhou Zhaolin, Xu Letian; General Affairs: Zhang Xianfang, Wang Jingdong, Zheng Dongshan; Reception: Zhou Fuzhang, Le Shuzi, Bing Jialiang, Chen Shude, Jin Weixuan, Sun Yinfeng, Xu Zhaozhou, Liang Gengshun, Yang Yongrun, Fan Tianjin, Qiu Xiliang, Lu Jiajun; Chief Investigator: Wu Jue, Xu Chengde, Liu Chunfan.

Welcome Scene

At around 1 p.m., Committee Member Chen Binghui prepared a car to go to Fenglinqiao to welcome the Panchen Lama to visit the exhibition. At 2:10 p.m., the Panchen Lama, accompanied by Secretary-General Liu Jiaju and Director of the Office Zhu Haishan, arrived at the exhibition accompanied by Chen Binghui. The military band dispatched by the Public Security Bureau in advance led the way and welcomed them into the auditorium, where they sat on the sofa prepared on the stage. At the same time, echoes were played to show respect. At 2:30 p.m., a welcome ceremony was held. First, Chairman Zhang Yichen delivered a welcome speech, followed by a reply speech by the Panchen Lama, and speeches by guests such as Wang Yansong.

(Photograph of the Panchen Lama Welcomed by the National Exhibition Hall (taken by Qichang Photo Studio)

After the presidium led the Panchen Lama and representatives of various government and military agencies and groups to visit the entire exhibition hall of national goods, the ceremony was completed after taking a photo at 3:30 p.m.

Chairman's Speech

At the National Goods Exhibition Hall's welcome to the Panchen Lama, Chairman Zhang Yichen said in his speech: "Today, we are honored to have the Panchen Lama visit and give a speech. All the members of our association are extremely happy and honored. The purpose of the National Exhibition Hall is to address the fact that in modern society, people admire Western culture and compete for luxury, leading to imported goods flooding the country and national goods being almost driven out. This is a great hidden worry for the future. Therefore, we have joined with colleagues to organize this association, on the one hand to resist the super-addition of imported goods, and on the other hand to regulate China's economy. Since the successive openings, we have been deeply grateful for the approval and joint maintenance of all sectors of society, and our reputation has increased day by day. If we can gradually promote and popularize it throughout the country, we may not be able to reverse the decline and increase the country's strength by one in ten thousand. The Lama is the Buddha of the West, a great man of our generation, who is concerned about national affairs and prays for peace, which is felt by the Chinese people. Wherever he goes, north and south, famous scholars and talented people rush to welcome him. On the day of his return, he will surely use the knowledge gained from his travels to govern the border people. Even if the powerful neighbors are concerned, it is difficult to achieve their ambitions of economic aggression. Today's welcome ceremony is like opening up another vital force for the future of production and sales cooperation of our national goods. I am writing this short speech to express my gratitude, and wish the party and the country ten thousand years, and the Lama ten thousand years."

Panchen Lama's Reply

After the chairman's speech, the Panchen Lama was invited to give a speech, which was translated by Secretary Liu Jiaji: "Today, I am very pleased to be invited to visit by the National Manufacturers Association. Your association promotes national goods in the spirit of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood. I am very grateful for the Panchen Lama's participation. After I return to Tibet, I will do my best to cooperate with you. Tibetan religion has a close relationship with politics and economy. In the future, I hope to work hard together to live and work in peace. China and the world are increasingly peaceful. Sun Yat-sen treats all races equally. I, the Panchen Lama, also uphold this purpose and wish the country prosperity day by day."

Wang Yansong's Speech

Then Wang Yansong gave a speech, saying: "The Panchen Lama has traveled from Ping to Nanjing, Hangzhou, and Shanghai this time. Wherever he goes, all groups and agencies welcome him sincerely. The meaning of the welcome from all walks of life and the relationship with Tibet have been published in newspapers, so there is no need to repeat them. Now, the Lama hopes that all sectors of China will become more peaceful and prosperous, but this is the common hope of the whole country. Our country is being forced by strong neighbors. Since the September 18th and January 28th incidents, the international background has become an open secret. Therefore, simply put, if we want to seek self-reliance, we must promote national goods. Because in recent years, the purchase of foreign goods and the outflow of money has been countless. They use our money to manufacture as much murderous weapon as possible in preparation for world war. The only remedy is not to buy foreign goods and not to overflow our rights and benefits. Everyone buys national goods.

Money will have nowhere to flow out. Now, when the master returns to Tibet, please do your best to promote and propagandize it. In the future, Tibet will be a huge source of goods for our country. If we do it with an indomitable spirit, we can achieve a rich country and a strong people, and live and work in peace." Then, Chen Jingsheng, the representative of the International Trade Bureau, gave a speech, and Liu Zhongying delivered a thank-you speech. The length of the speeches will not be recorded.

Week-Long Visit

were security teams in charge of investigation, and anyone with suspicious behavior was prohibited from entering. Therefore, the security in the venue was very strict.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a petition to the municipal government, stating: "The purpose of this petition is as follows: On the 6th of this month, we received a letter from the Wusong branch of our association, stating that during the typhoon last year, the seawall of Wusong was washed away in more than a dozen places along the coast and along the harbor. The mud dike on the north side collapsed for tens of feet, and the situation is even more dangerous. Our office has reported to your association and urgently requested the authorities to come and repair it. We were informed that we have telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government to allocate funds for it. However, after a year, the breach in the Wusong seawall remains and the provincial government has not sent workers to repair it. Now that the summer flood season is about to pass and the autumn tides are following, it is inevitable that the broken seawall will be overwhelmed by the endless wind and waves, and the breach will expand and flood the people of Wusong. Our office is taking precautions and taking care of the lives of the people of Wusong, and we cannot sit idly by. Therefore, we ask your association to transfer the matter to the municipal authorities and ask the Public Works Bureau to quickly repair the collapsed sections of the outer road of Wusong and the mud dike on the north side as soon as possible, so that the people of Wusong will be fortunate. After investigation, Wusong Town is under the jurisdiction of our city, and the seawall project is related to the lives of the people of Wusong. The year-long repair project is equivalent to building a house on the road. The summer flood season is approaching, and looking ahead, we are terrified. We hereby submit this petition to your office for verification and approval, and request that the Public Works Bureau be instructed to allocate funds quickly to repair the collapsed sections of the outer road of the town and the mud dike on the north side as soon as possible, so as to protect the lives of millions of people in the town. Declaration by the Newspaper Trade Union: In Support of the Striking Workers of the Anglo-American Tobacco Factory

Fellow countrymen across the nation! The more someone wears the mask of civilization, the more barbarous and unreasonable their actions become. This is especially true of British imperialists. We cannot help but recall the May 30th Massacre of 1925, where they slaughtered countless innocent compatriots in their eagerness to curry favor with Japanese capitalists. At that time, we passively resisted by implementing a "boycott of enemy goods," but that brief burst of enthusiasm has long since faded away. Yet their methods of aggression have made remarkable progress since then.

Let's take a look at how tyrannical the capitalists of the Anglo-American Tobacco Company are. They use extraterritoriality as a shield, setting aside the orders of Chinese officials, and dismissing the three thousand-odd workers who produce for them with the flimsy excuse of "poor business and worker insubordination." On May 12th, they abruptly announced the factory's closure, condemning workers who have contributed to the company's success to death. Everyone knows that the Anglo-American Tobacco Company's profits are staggeringly high. As such, they should treat the workers who produce for them with sweat and blood with generosity. However, the reality is quite the opposite.

Of course, we do not dream that these "robbers will have a change of heart," but we hope they will maintain the status quo, so that a group of toiling workers can continue to make a living. As for the claim of worker insubordination, that is even more of a joke. If it were indeed true, the company could file a complaint with the Chinese authorities, who have methods for dealing with such situations. However, the company authorities have not considered this. Instead, they suddenly resort to high-handed tactics against our group of intellectually unsophisticated, desperate laborers. They recklessly undermine the amity between the two nations and hire a large number of armed detectives to beat and injure over a dozen defenseless fellow workers.

Let us now be blunt: the Anglo-American Tobacco Company's capitalists are not motivated by poor business or worker insubordination. Rather, the Anglo-American Tobacco Company authorities are deliberately sabotaging the labor movement in our country and resent the high wages of the original workers. They seek to replace them with another group of workers, subject to their exploitation, to satiate their selfish desires for economic aggression.

Finally, we hope that our government authorities will not treat this strike as just another ordinary labor dispute. If the Anglo-American Tobacco Company is allowed to oppress in this manner, we believe that many similar labor disputes will soon follow. The Newspaper Trade Union, bearing the principles of "when the lips are gone, the teeth are cold" and "shared destiny," cannot bear to stand idly by while a group of toiling workers cry out in hunger and cold, suffering the devastation of imperialism, without taking action. We hope that countrymen across the nation will provide unified assistance to achieve ultimate victory. This declaration is hereby made.

Gaoyou: Completion of Six Breaches in Stone Embankment Undertaken by the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee; Provincial Government Dispatches Personnel for Inspection and Acceptance

The Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee at 97 Renji Road previously consulted with the Jiangsu Provincial Government regarding the repair of breaches in the Gaoyou Canal dike at locations such as the Tangjunlou Miaoxiangkou and the Qigongdian, and the conversion of earthen dikes into stone structures. Recognizing this as an important measure for disaster prevention, it was decided at several meetings to undertake the project, and Huang Hanzhi was publicly appointed as the director, and Wang Shuxiang as the deputy director of the project. The planned charts and diagrams were submitted to the Provincial Government for record, and construction continued. The dike is four zhang high, six zhang wide, and 1,522 chi long. The project took ten months and was completely finished last month. The Provincial Government appointed Secretary Shen Bao and Technician Sun Fengwu of the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau to represent them in the inspection and acceptance on June 1st in Gaoyou. The measured dimensions of height, width, and length were all in excess, and the workmanship was up to standard. It was also said that in the 700 li of the canal south from Jiangkou and north to the Shandong border, there had never been such a project. This demonstrates that the work is solid, the materials are reliable, and the management is competent. If the receiving agency can properly maintain and protect it in the years to come, then the lives and property of millions of people in the ten counties of Jiangbei can be protected from the threat of flooding.

Results of the Tiger Brand Yong An Tang Appeal: Ren An Tang's Monkey and Lion Trademarks Revoked

Since Tiger Brand Yong An Tang's medicines were introduced to the country, their effectiveness and remarkable efficacy have led to increased sales and a growing reputation. As a result, some unscrupulous individuals have tried various methods to imitate the brand in order to profit. Shantou Ren An Tang is one of them, having used the lion and monkey trademarks to imitate Tiger Brand's Wan Jin You and Bagua Dan, etc. Yong An Tang filed a lawsuit according to law, resulting in a prison sentence and the approval of the Trademark Bureau to revoke its monkey and lion trademarks. After repeated litigation, the Executive Yuan finally decided to uphold the Trademark Bureau's decision to revoke Ren An Tang's monkey and lion trademarks. The decision is recorded below to inform those concerned about trademark disputes:

Executive Yuan Decision Letter No. 19, Twenty-Third Year, Su Zi: Re-Appellant Hu Wenhua's Agent Hu Guigeng of Tiger Brand Yong An Tang. The right re-appellant, in the case of the dispute with Ren An Tang over the monkey and lion trademarks, was dissatisfied with the decision of the Ministry of Industry and filed a re-appeal. The decision of this Yuan is as follows:

"Main Text" The original decision is revoked. The Trademark Bureau's decision to revoke Ren An Tang's monkey and monkey trademarks is upheld.

"Facts" The re-appellant claimed that Ren An Tang Pharmacy had added images and text to the approved Trademark Bureau registration No. 15967 monkey trademark and No. 17953 running lion trademark, imitating the re-appellant's registered Tiger, Bagua Dan, approved portrait and graphics of Hu Wenhua and Hu Wenbao, and filed a petition to the Trademark Bureau for revocation in July 1931. After ordering Ren An Tang to respond repeatedly, Ren An Tang stated in a submission to the office on March 21, 1932 (the original decision and re-appeal letter mistakenly stated March 17, 1932) that it was willing to cease using the added annotations on the monkey and lion trademarks from that day forward. The existing packaged goods, all with added images and text around the monkey trademark and running lion trade name, would be destroyed. The bureau approved this and notified the re-appellant. On September 23, 1932, the re-appellant submitted multiple illustrations as proof that Ren An Tang's disputed trademark annotations had not been destroyed and continued to be used, infringing on trademark exclusive rights, and requested the Trademark Bureau to revoke the trademarks. The bureau then, in accordance with Article 19 of the Trademark Law, revoked the registration of the monkey and lion trademarks with Order No. 5231. Ren An Tang, dissatisfied with this decision, appealed to the Ministry of Industry on the grounds that it had not continued to use the annotations. The ministry then decided to revoke the original decision of the Trademark Bureau. The re-appellant, unwilling to accept the decision, filed a re-appeal with this Yuan.

"Reasoning" To determine whether there is merit to this re-appeal, it must be determined whether Ren An Tang continued to use the monkey and lion trademark annotations after March 20, 1932. According to the emergency notice submitted by the re-appellant on September 20, 1933, from Zhangzhou Shunxing and other shops, it stated, "Our shop and others sell Lion Brand Panacea." The apology notice from Lin Zhenxun, the owner of Xiamen Zhaoyuan Pharmacy, stated, "Our pharmacy recently consigned Lion Brand Panacea from Guo Dongcai of Shantou Ren An Tang." Furthermore, the judgment document Yi Zi No. 361 of the Minhou Local Court on November 14, 1933, recognized in its fact section that Zhou Wudi purchased 87 dozen of Ren An Tang's imitations of Yong An Tang's Tiger Brand Wan Jin You on April 10 of the same year, convicting Zhou Wudi of the crime of "selling goods with counterfeit trademarks." Therefore, the re-appellant's claim that Ren An Tang continued to use the annotations of the aforementioned trademarks after March 21, 1932, is credible. The Trademark Bureau, in accordance with the provisions of Article 19, Paragraph 1, Item 1 of the Trademark Law, revoked the registration of Ren An Tang's monkey and lion trademarks, and there is nothing wrong with it. The Ministry of Industry's revocation of the original decision cannot be considered appropriate. Based on the above reasoning, this re-appeal is justified. Therefore, in accordance with the first paragraph of Article 9 of the Administrative Appeal Law, it is decided as in the main text.

President Wang Zhaoming, May 16, Twenty-Third Year

When she was unable to live separately, she committed suicide by hanging herself. However, because there were injuries on her body after death, Qiu Chuanlang sued in the original county, alleging murder, claiming that she was beaten to death and then hanged to cover up the crime. The original county examined the body and ruled it a suicide, dismissing the case. Qiu, dissatisfied, appealed to the High Court, which appointed the Shanghai Local Court to re-examine the body. After sending it to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for autopsy, the result was that although Qiu Yin Xian died by hanging, there were minor injuries on her body. The prosecutor still dismissed the case against Yang Miaolang. Qiu Chuanlang, because there were injuries on his daughter's body, claimed that those responsible for the injuries should also be held accountable. He continued to appeal to the High Court, which sent it back for further investigation. Yesterday, the case was convened, and the official ordered Yang Miaolang to be detained pending legal action. When Qiu Chuanlang heard the order, he said that his daughter's grievances had been redressed and he could die without regret.

No Ghosts in the New House in Hua'anfang 丨Our Reporter's Investigation Reveals the Truth丨 Three Cement Workers Died of Gas Poisoning After Accidentally Damaging a Gas Pipe, But Rumormongers Created False Stories to Deceive the Public

Since the night before last, rumors have been rampant that strange and ghostly events have suddenly occurred in the city house at No. 35, Hua'anfang New House, Huaxing Road, North Zhejiang Road. The rumors spread far and wide, and people rushed to investigate, as if it were true. However, when asked for details, no one could provide any proof. Therefore, after an investigation by this newspaper, it was concluded that the rumors were undoubtedly fabricated by mischief-makers, or perhaps there were other motives for creating such unfounded tales to confuse people. However, it is true that two carpenters and one cement worker died suddenly in the house. When a certain grocery store was about to move in, they found that the floorboards were not properly laid, so they hired them to re-lay the floor. The original floorboards were removed, and the cement workers dug into the ground. Seeing that the soil underneath was uneven, they used a nail bar to turn it over. Unexpectedly, there was an old gas pipe buried there. The cement had corroded the pipe, making it old and worn. The carpenters, unaware of this, struck the pipe too hard with the bar, breaking it. The gas immediately rushed out, and the three of them were the first to be hit, collapsing instantly. No one noticed what happened afterward. By the time they were discovered, they had all suffocated to death due to the prolonged exposure to the gas. At the same time, the grocery store, considering it a bad omen, also canceled the move. This is the true story. Unexpectedly, a group of idlers fabricated the facts, spread rumors to deceive the public, and spoke with certainty, as if they had witnessed it themselves. And the ignorant common people, without considering the credibility of the rumors, spread them from person to person, deceiving themselves and others. Perhaps there is another purpose behind this, which is beyond their comprehension. Fortunately, Gong Xi-kui, the district chief of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau of Zhabei, and the Huishi Police Station have both understood the situation. Therefore, in addition to dispatching detectives to secretly investigate the rumormongers and arrest and punish them severely, they have also dispatched armed detectives and regular police to suppress the situation day and night to prevent unscrupulous or reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to cause trouble. At the same time, District Chief Gong will separately investigate and then submit for legal action against the more than ten rioters who were detained for taking the opportunity to cause trouble, beating police officers, and tearing their uniforms on the evening of the sixth (the day before yesterday) in order to maintain public order.

The Truth About Sprinkling Corrosive Acid That Led to Death, Animosity Resulting From Revising An Unacceptable Contract, The Father Died in Anger, The Son Held a Grudge and Sought Revenge

Shi Jixiang, a native of Jiangbei, was suddenly splashed with nitric acid at around 9:00 PM on the 2nd of last month in front of the Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road, causing serious injuries. He was taken to the hospital but died on the 10th despite treatment. After someone reported it to the Putuo Road Police Station, it was found that Dong Qingtian, a worker at the Nisshin Cotton Spinning Factory No. 2, was suspected of being involved in the case. While they were investigating, Dong heard about the incident and surrendered to the police station with his lawyer, Song Shixiang. The next morning, he was escorted to the First Special Court, where he denied the charges. He was ordered to be detained pending further investigation. The case has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, it was time for the continuation of the interrogation, but the defendant had already fully confessed to the police station, so the police station officially filed a lawsuit in accordance with Article 296 of the Criminal Law for injury resulting in death. Judge Xiao Xie-fen presided over the interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Court. The defendant hired lawyers Fan Gang and Song Shixiang to defend him. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the police station stated that the defendant had confessed everything to the police station since the last postponement. As for why he committed such a murder, the matter was trivial and would not be condoned by wise people. Shi Yisheng (the nephew of the deceased), the defendant's brother-in-law, wanted to return to his native Jiangbei to purchase land two years ago and entrusted the defendant's father, Dong Shangbei, to write all the contracts. However, because the wording was inadequate, Shi asked the deceased to review them, and the deceased deemed them unsuitable and revised them. The defendant's father was very dissatisfied, considering it a great insult, and fell ill from anger, eventually dying. Before his death, he told his son, the defendant, that his death was caused by the deceased. Therefore, the defendant held a grudge and committed the murder. On the 1st of last month, the defendant went to the Nisshin Anbu Iron Factory at No. 1034, Lane 44, Gordon Road, and obtained half a bottle of nitric acid from Guo Xiaowuzi, a rickshaw puller, and took it home. At around 7:00 PM the next night, the defendant passed by his brother-in-law Shi Yisheng's house at No. 962 Binlang Road and saw the deceased having dinner. Knowing that the deceased had to pass by Xiaoshadu Road after dinner, he rushed home, got the nitric acid, and hid behind a telephone pole in front of the Labor Hospital. When the deceased and his friend arrived there, the defendant unexpectedly reached out and splashed the acid, then turned around and fled without a trace. The deceased died several days later due to severe injuries. Afterward, the defendant felt guilty and asked for leave from the factory to flee to Wuxi. It was not until the 30th of last month that the defendant surrendered to the police station with his lawyer, Song. At first, he firmly denied the charges, hoping to deceive the authorities, but in the end, the police station found out the facts and summoned various witnesses to testify. The defendant then fully confessed. Now there are nine witnesses, including Shi Jinian, Liu Xitang, and Shi Derun, who can prove that they witnessed the defendant splashing the acid and everything that happened. Then, each witness testified one by one. When questioned, the defendant also confessed to the above situation. After the lawyers on both sides debated, Judge Xiao ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody pending sentencing on Thursday next week.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Plans to Build a Cemetery for Police Officers Who Died in the Line of Duty, The Address Is Set in Western Shanghai, Covering an Area of Twenty Mu, Construction Will Begin as Soon as the Funds Are Raised

The Municipal Public Security Bureau is commemorating police officers who died in the line of duty by constructing a monument to them at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Hongxing Road in Zhabei. The unveiling will take place soon. Details have been reported in various newspapers. According to the reporter of Shenshi News Agency's inquiry to the Public Security Bureau, in addition to the monument, there are plans to construct a cemetery for police officers who died in the line of duty. In the past, the families of police officers who died in the line of duty or died from overwork received considerable compensation, but their remains were either unable to be transported back to their hometowns or were scattered in various places, which was not ideal. Therefore, the plan is to build a cemetery to commemorate them and comfort their souls. The address of the cemetery has been selected in western Shanghai, covering an area of approximately twenty mu. During construction, it is planned to surround it with bamboo fences or stone railings, plant pine and cypress trees, and erect a beautifully carved stone archway at the entrance. In the center of the cemetery, a white stone altar will be set up, connected by a path. On both sides will be police officers' tombs, arranged according to surname, so that family members can easily find them when they come to pay their respects. After the cemetery is completed, in addition to transferring all the remains of the already buried police officers, extra spaces will be reserved for future deaths in the line of duty. During important seasons, the bureau will send personnel to sweep and pay respects. The entire project is expected to cost approximately 80,000 to 90,000 yuan. The bureau has already raised 50,000 yuan and is actively raising funds. Construction will begin as soon as the funds are sufficient. ×××

At that time, a stray bullet hit an elderly woman buying vegetables in the chest, causing profuse bleeding and serious injuries. Afterward, the French Police called an ambulance to rush the injured woman to the hospital for treatment. Her life is in critical condition. The other six bandits took the opportunity to escape from the rooftops and other places. The two captured bandits were taken back for interrogation, and they confessed the names of many accomplices. The investigation is currently underway.

After reviewing the statements, Judge Wu Fang-lian ordered the hearing to be postponed for ten days and the defendant to be summoned to court again. He also ordered Cai to submit to a forensic examination to verify the injuries.

The Jardine Matheson's Changjiang class Lianhe ship, which was traveling from Shanghai to Hankou, damaged its engine when it struck a rock mid-journey. The ship was unable to continue to Hankou. The cargo and passengers have been transferred to the Longhe wheel. The Lianhe wheel returned to Shanghai for major repairs. The details are as follows:

The Lianhe wheel of Jardine Matheson

Damaged Wheel departed from Shanghai on the 5th of this month to transport cargo to Hankou. Because Dasheng Yarn Factory in Nantong had a batch of cotton yarn to be shipped to Hankou on the ship, the Lianhe wheel stopped in Tongzhou to load the yarn. After loading was completed, the ship left Nantong. When raising the anchor, it was necessary to turn the ship around. There are many shallow sandbars and reefs in this area, making it very difficult to turn the ship. The Lianhe accidentally, the engine blade at the stern of the ship, collided with a rock on the riverbank. Fortunately, the wheel was a twin-engine wheel, and one blade was destroyed on the spot, but it was still able to continue sailing.

Continued, After the engine blade of the wheel was damaged, because there was still

Town, The wheel could barely operate with one blade, but the speed had been greatly reduced, making it difficult to reach Hankou. The ship owner telegraphed the Shanghai office for instructions and was allowed to sail to Zhenjiang, transfer the cargo and passengers, and return to Shanghai for major repairs. The Lianhe wheel sailed from Tongzhou to Zhenjiang and anchored to wait. The company's Longhe wheel went upstream to Zhenjiang. The cargo and passengers of Lianhe were transferred to the Longhe, which continued to Hankou. The Lianhe was emptied and returned to Shanghai.

This afternoon, The Shanghai office received a telegram from Zhenjiang yesterday afternoon, indicating that the Lianhe's cargo and passengers had been completely transferred to the Longhe, transported to Hankou, and would sail back to Shanghai from Zhenjiang that evening. Because the journey was delayed, it was expected to enter the port this afternoon. After arriving in Shanghai, the company will inspect the extent of the damage and then proceed to dock for repairs. Zhang Naiqi Discusses Man and Environment

The Chinese Staff Association of the Public Works Department held its second academic lecture yesterday at the Public Works Department Hygiene Sub-Office at No. 340 Hankou Road. They invited Mr. Zhang Naiqi, President of the China Industrial Bank, to lecture on Man and Environment. More than one hundred people attended. Jin Baisheng presided over the meeting, and Bingxun Stenography Society took shorthand notes. The lecture stated that man and environment are like heroes and times. Examples like the Seven Swords and Thirteen Knights from the ancient book "Water Margin" and modern figures like Mussolini and Hitler can all be considered heroes, but these are reactionary heroes of despotism, dictatorship, jumping over walls, and throwing bombs, which are not in line with the times. Generally, people are often influenced by historical education and heroism, so they often have the word "hero" in their minds, but each person's view of a hero is different. However, whether a hero can create the times or the times create a hero is a matter of debate. Most young people believe that a hero can create the times, but once they enter society, they feel the difficulty of transforming the times. Some people believe that a hero cannot create the times, but the times can create a hero, meaning that people are limited by their environment and that a hero has no place to use his talents if the time is not right. This kind of statement is just a general excuse for unsuccessful people to cover up their own faults and console themselves. Modern ethical science says that although a person's future is subject to the environment, a person's efforts can advance the environment, meaning that although a person's path is determined by the environment, a person can shorten the route through effort. This theory is very accurate. Therefore, we should use the environment, advance the environment, and within the realm of possibility, not let the opportunity pass. Hu Shi said that China would not perish in fifty years, and Japan would perish on its own. Zhang Boquan said that Japan would have a revolution and perish on its own in ten years. If China strives to advance, then the day of Japan's demise will come sooner, and China can be revived earlier. This is the meaning of times and heroes, that is, man and environment.
