Shen Bao This Port Supplement

Talk

Reason

— He Juefu

It is said that northerners value reason the most. If you give him a scolding or a few slaps, he will first ask you if you are being reasonable. If you can clearly state the great reason why you are treating him this way, then he will silently endure it and admit his bad luck. Otherwise, he will risk his entire life to fight with you to the death, no matter the cost.

Originally, a person who disregards everything for the sake of respecting reason is worthy of admiration and praise. But this also sufficiently reveals his foolishness and stupidity, because he simply does not understand that reason is originally a slippery thing.

The story of a person who secretly rides the ruler's chariot because his mother is sick, and offers the remaining peaches to the ruler to win the ruler's praise, but is killed as a result, is known to everyone. Up until now, the changes in events have become even more bizarre: clearly killing and arson is called maintaining world peace; clearly seizing and occupying by force is called good neighborliness. For many years, every time a major or minor incident has occurred, has it not been based on a great reason? Pitifully, a group of people who adhere to reason have silently and quietly endured humiliation and injustice under this.

The level of civilization of a country is often measured by the degree to which the people of that country abide by reason. Because everyone is reasonable, then barbarism is completely shed, and there are no cases of the strong oppressing the weak or the many bullying the few, and the world is at peace. Our country has thousands of years of history, and our people have undergone such a long period of tempering and edification, so the degree to which they adhere to reason will naturally be higher than that of others. But, unfortunately, it is precisely because our country is the most reasonable country, speaking reason to the extreme and making everything logical, so there are still inevitably those who suffer losses and injustices without realizing it. Not being reasonable at all is certainly not good, but completely believing in reason is also very dangerous!

International Labour Conference

— Qiong Sheng

Recently, on the shores of Lake Geneva in Geneva, the League of Nations Administrative Council, Advisory Committee, Disarmament and other conferences have been bustling, and the world's politicians, diplomats, and experts have been constantly gathering in the "Palace of Peace." Like a continuous stream of carriages on Shanyin Road, it was quite a grand scene for a time. While these events are still "echoing" in our minds, the International Labour Conference, attended by representatives from forty-six countries, has opened with great ceremony amidst the reflections of the lake. This place has always been filled and occupied by important figures on the world political stage. Everyone knows that it is for "upholding justice and striving for peace," which goes without saying. Now, the so-called "worker representatives" from various countries are competing with each other and gathering here to discuss matters, which naturally deserves our attention. The development of the labor movement, especially the manifestation of international solidarity among the working class, is enough to make those from the increasingly declining classes gasp in astonishment when mentioned even briefly, because the progress of this situation will inevitably raise the issue of the actual improvement of the lives of the working masses themselves, as well as the issue of changing the existing social system that is incompatible with improving their own lives. However, the proposal and advancement of these events must be met head-on by those in various countries who are concerned about social order. However, the League of Nations "Labour" Conference can hold its eighteenth regular meeting in a grand manner on the banks of the Geneva River, which is its unique feature and cannot be regarded as just another labor conference.

In the current situation of deepening economic panic and increasingly urgent war crises, on the one hand, laborers are suffering from wage cuts, increased working hours, starvation, and unemployment; on the other hand, they are painfully aware of losing their freedom to survive and being forced to be "cannon fodder." If this statement is true, and it is generally recognized, then the thorough resolution of these events is the current task of laborers and the "workers' interests" that must be strived for unanimously. In that case, how will these representatives of the International Labour Conference discuss and debate in the "Palace of Peace" to seek the well-being of the workers on these issues?

According to a Geneva dispatch: "Matters related to the interests of world laborers will be brought up for discussion: ··· The main agenda item is the plan to alleviate world unemployment: ··· and promote large-scale public works to reduce unemployment. Supporters of the forty-hour work week will urge the final reading of the forty-hour work week draft. The conference will also submit the draft of unemployment insurance and other assistance to unemployed workers for final reading," and so on. In these agendas, it can be seen that the representatives of the conference also believe that unemployment is a serious situation in the world at the moment, making many rulers of the current society dizzy, but they are limited by the aura of their own "colored glasses," intentionally or unable to see through this situation, revealing the problem of the social organization that causes unemployment. Therefore, the International Labour Conference can only treat the symptom but not the cause, and without any actual implementation, read out the draft of unemployment insurance and other assistance to unemployed workers again and again. As for the forty-hour work week, although "labor experts" say that it does not conflict with the new industry regulations in the United States, with the opposition of the United Kingdom, "it is not believed that it can pass the meeting," which is even more of a case of "discussion without a decision."

The essence of this "main agenda" of the International Labour Conference is such, so even if the conference re-elects the "Committee to Protect the Interests of Workers," even if it is believed that it will "pass the meeting," it is not seen that it can truly "protect the interests of workers." As for the "highly instructive" effect on Germany, which will be used to apply for "public works" to be built in various countries, regardless of anything else, we know that Hitler's war preparations have been very enthusiastic recently, and the military industry is extremely developed. The United States, Britain, France, Japan, and others are also doing the same. Is this the "public works" of the International Labour Conference to alleviate unemployment? Its solution to unemployment!

The International Labour Conference is convened by the Labour Bureau of the League of Nations. Among its twenty-four elected administrative personnel, twelve are government representatives from various countries, six are worker representatives, and six are employer representatives. This is why the International Labour Conference is the International Labour Conference.

Words from the Model Society

— Xi Zhen

Friends:

From your letter, I can roughly see a self-portrait of your distress; from education, from knowledge, from scholars' books, from professors' dictation, you have established an ideal future that is perfect in every way; and you have taken this ideal, if you keep it locked in a house, keep it immersed in the embrace of others, keep it buried in the outline of general theories, then there will be no problem. Now you have bumped into reality, bumped into it until your skin is broken and your bones are cracked, which was originally an expected thing and is not surprising. When iron is thrown into a furnace to be forged, it may not be a pleasant thing for the iron itself; moreover, the lesson you have learned is only the first chapter of the introduction arranged for you by the teacher of reality?

You say that you feel that everything in this world is a bit wrong, and everything is a bit unsatisfactory; and when it comes to this "not quite right" and "unsatisfactory," you can't find the source of its disease, and the treatment is of course out of the question. "Discovering the unsatisfactory and having to live in this helpless unsatisfactory is the 'most painful thing'." As you said; however, knowing the reason, knowing the solution, if you lack the power to act, it will also make you annoyed, have you ever thought about this? You asked me about the reason for your烦闷 and the solution, but I can't tell you anything. Regarding this, you should ask American-style Chinese professors who are good at compiling lecture outlines, or youth guidance experts, they will definitely recite 1234 and ABCD fluently to you item by item, although whether the reason is right or not, whether the method is useful or not is a question, but they are still a guide; and my age is almost the same as yours, I am still groping in the dark, and I can't find a concrete way to relieve my distress: and sometimes, I can't help but be as depressed as you are. For your "seeking a panacea" style of desire, can I bear to give you incense ash and rotten candle oil that I don't know to make a elixir?

However, precisely because I am also patiently drinking the bitter wine of youth like you, and I am treading on dangerous waves; and now, I have been thrown into the white-hot fire; and we often talk together, talking about everything. I think the person who knows a person best is no one else but himself, then my observation and understanding of you, or can be said to be ourselves knowing ourselves?

I can't say anything else to you, but there is one phenomenon that makes me deeply puzzled, that is: you worship fate too much, and you believe in opportunity too much: therefore, you have doubts and distrust about yourself. However, opportunity and fate often pull people away from reality, and what you see and experience are all the ugliest aspects of reality, and your ideals and body are growing contradictorily in you.

Is this the source of our tragedy?

In me, from hunger, from the daily planning for survival, from the battle of the masses for life, I have learned a new lesson, deeply believing that people are not easily despised animals; only in this way, I am not willing to despise myself.

Believing in yourself does not necessarily mean doubting others, I suppose there is no need to say more about this?

However, in this era, people like you may be tolerated by the general society, because they are asking people to abandon reality to pursue opportunity, to pursue fate. Is the "Hamlet" type of youth who is hesitant and accomplishes nothing not considered to be well-behaved? There are many people in this era who are enticing people with opportunities. If you can't believe in yourself and still indulge in opportunity and fate, then I advise you to buy more aviation lottery tickets, maybe you will win a first prize.

Otherwise, there is only one other way to go: believe in yourself. But no matter which way you go丨丨buy lottery tickets or believe in yourself, I sincerely wish you success.

Talking About Prison Life

— Li Kui

Everyone is afraid of prison life. Because once a free "person" enters prison, they become an unfree "object." Like a bird in a cage; the door is locked all day long, and there is no sunlight in the room. Eating, living, and moving all take place in a small room, which is so terrible! However, in addition to being terrible, it makes people reluctant to leave. Although I decided not to go back to prison life after I came out; the impression that prison life gave me is very good. At least it makes me very nostalgic for life in prison. Really. The impression that prison gave me is not very terrible.

Although the food in prison is easy to get sick from, although staying in prison for a long time can easily turn a good person into a cripple, into a dead person! But in terms of spirit, one can indeed get comfort that one cannot get outside. This comfort can almost make people forget the suffering they are enduring.

You can find real friends in prison. Prison is a small society: but the hypocrisy and coldness that exists in the larger society are not present here. Because they are all under the same oppression.

If someone inflicts unreasonable persecution on us, we will resist it together. If we fail, everyone is sad; if we win, we will hug each other and dance. Really, we are not divided from each other.

Prison is full of pure love, innocent love. We are so natural: if we want to hug, we hug to our heart's content: if we want to kiss, we kiss to our heart's content; no one laughs at us, and no one interferes: we are truly melting in the furnace of great love.

Really, this kind of natural love cannot be found outside; just like me and A Qiu, we often hugged inside; now when we meet, apart from shaking hands, there is no purer expression.

Life in prison is full of true love, if you are inevitably dragged there, don't be afraid! It can give you things that you can't get outside.

Miscellany

— Yi Li

The rice bowl of the poor is equal to the toilet of the rich.

The buttocks of modern women are as respected as the faces and mouths of wealthy people.

The words spoken by the disempowered mouth are as useless as the garbage in a trash can, and the spittle flowing from the mouth of the triumphant is as noble as the shad in May.

When poor people die, having a son is like having no son; when wealthy people die, even if they have no son, they can still have many descendants.

In life, it is better to die than to be poor.

Women in the lower and middle classes of Shanghai, even if they have never read a book in their lives, they can always recognize dozens of characters. What is the reason? Because they remember the east, west, north, and south in mahjong, as well as the thirty-six gates of playing huahui, only dozens of characters, which they remember by heart.

When children are just learning to speak, they know how to scold people.

Human Relationships are Cold and Warm

— Guang Han

Who doesn't sigh and say, "Human relationships are cold and warm!" When a person is prominent, everyone will respect them. Once this person unfortunately fails, there is a feeling of separation from the world, and they will be met with contempt everywhere. Conversely, a person who is in trouble will be looked down upon. Occasionally, if they have good luck, their value will naturally rise. What is the reason for this? Because the person is different before and after. Here, it fully illustrates that people are opportunistic. Because they are opportunistic, they must worship the rich and powerful. They must despise the poor.

In fact, people may not be different. When they are rich and powerful, they are this person. When they are poor, they are still this person. The only difference is the environment that supports this person. And a group of sycophants, what they worship is not this person, but this person's position and power. What they despise is not this person, but this person's tattered clothes.

However, position and power are other people's position and power, which have nothing to do with oneself, so why worship them? Because worshiping them often brings benefits, so why not do it? As for tattered clothes, they are other people's tattered clothes, which do not hinder oneself, so why despise them? This is a bit difficult to say. Apart from guarding against them coming to complain and beg for mercy, there is only disgust to explain it.

People are always opportunistic. Human relationships are always cold and warm. I think, if there is a person who goes from triumph to failure, on this road, they can taste two different flavors of life, and also recognize two different faces of the world!

Sorrow

— Shu Hao

The floating clouds were running wildly in the sky, and the leaves of the梧桐tree made rustling sounds as they were blown by the wind. The terrifying god of night had executed his authority, covering the earth with a dark curtain. At this time, the surroundings were as silent as death, with only a few dying autumn insects whimpering intermittently. It was dark and oppressive, and nothing could be seen, but looking eastward, there was a faint light shining straight from a small house. From the broken window gap, everything in the room could be vaguely seen. This was a small building that was not even a square foot in size. In the center was a dilapidated desk, covered with untidy books, with writing brushes, fountain pens, and ink scattered in the middle. Next to it was a low stool and a military bed. A kerosene lamp hung in the center of the room, and the faint light came from there. A thin youth, with his face in his hands, disheveled hair, draped over his eyebrows, was sitting on the stool, burying his entire head in his arms. Suddenly, he sighed slowly, and at the same time, he moved his hands, placing them crossed on the table, and slightly raised his head, staring blankly at the dimly lit kerosene lamp. He was saddened by the autumn night seven years ago when his father took his last breath. A happy family was shrouded in sorrow from then on. His poor mother and young sister had gone to their distant hometown due to the pressure of life. And he, without the ability to be independent, had to struggle under the iron hooves of life. He shook his head, unable to continue thinking, and two shining tears flowed down from his eyes.

Amateur Mailbox

Have You Grown Distant From Your Original Family? ·

Editor:

I am a 19-year-old youth, currently working in a customs brokerage firm in this port. My native place is Kunshan, and my family only has a loving mother and a young sister. In addition, there is an elder brother and a sister-in-law.

Page 21

My elder brother is doing business in Wuxi, but he has not had any children. About a month ago, a relative mentioned my marriage and introduced me to be a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family. I didn't say anything at the time. Frankly speaking, my environment does not have the ability to marry a wife, but I don't think there is a need to marry a wife, so I have never been bothered by it. Now, asking me to distance myself from my original family, including my loving mother, elder brother, and sister, and go to be a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family is definitely not what I want, but I can't say any specific reasons for objecting other than that. If my mother and others agree that I should go to be a son-in-law, what method should I take? Sir! What do you think is the right way to handle this? I am willing to do anything in case of unavoidable circumstances. Please reply in the newspaper! I am looking forward to it very much. Sincerely wish you well! Ai Jianan.

Answer: I don't know why you are afraid of being a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family. "Distancing yourself from your original family" is your excessive worry, and this is not a reason. Although a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family has to live in his wife's family, his wife's family will never limit the son-in-law's actions and prevent you from approaching your "original family." Whether you are "distant" or "close" to your family depends entirely on yourself, and others cannot force it. You think that you must live in the family to be considered close to the family, which is a big mistake. Such a distance is inevitable for men, and it will not only happen when you become a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family. You are now working in Shanghai, and according to your letter, your family seems to be still in your native place. Isn't this a distance from your family? Therefore, it is not enough for you to oppose being a son-in-law solely on the basis of "distance." The issues that marriage becomes are whether the man and woman get along and the burden of marriage in the future. You should also consider these two points for the marriage introduced by your relative this time. Whether or not to be a son-in-law who lives with his wife's family is not a problem in my opinion. Editor

Travelogue

Impressions of Chang'an

— Yunshan

In the third month of spring, I took a trip to the Northwest. I took a train from the capital, Nanjing, passed through the temporary capital, Luoyang, and reached Tongguan. Then, I took a car and went straight to the accompanying capital, Xi'an.

Xi'an is the ancient Chang'an: also known as Xijing. The impressions that I am now preparing to describe have nothing to do with major issues concerning the national economy and people's livelihood. Let the "experts" who develop the Northwest elaborate on their grand theories! My so-called impressions are just like this:

1. Mud in Sunny and Rainy Weather

"Three feet of dust without wind, a street of mud with rain," this is a famous line used by people in the past to ridicule the streets of Beijing. If it is transferred to the ancient road of Chang'an, it will be even more so! The "dust" and "mud" of Chang'an do have their special material basis.

Most of the streets in this ancient city are primitive dirt roads. The Northwest, where there is not much rainfall in ordinary times, is originally prone to dust and sand. In addition, old-fashioned carts are constantly rolling all day long, and long-distance buses are running back and forth. The yellow dust flying all over the city is naturally even more spectacular! If there is a bit of wind, then "the sun and moon will be dim, and the mountains and rivers will change color!"

The mud here is different from other places. First, it is rich in viscosity; second, it is because of the rolling of trains and cars, the road becomes muddy after a rain!

Because the soil is rich in viscosity, the streets often turn into "mud pools" after heavy rain, and you can actually walk on dry shoes on both sides of the road! However, you have to be careful and follow the existing footprints on the road: concentrate your mind! You can't be careless at all; otherwise, there is a risk of slipping into the "mud pool."

Film Supplement

Friday, June 8, 23rd Year of the Republic of China

The Shun Pao Screen Section

A Sensational Hide-and-Seek in Hollywood: The Peculiar Temperament of Universal Starlet Margaret Sullavan (Part 1)

— Jia Mo

Margaret Sullavan, the new female star of Universal Pictures, made a stunning debut with her first film, "Only Yesterday." Its public release garnered praise from audiences worldwide. In Shanghai, it played at the Nanjing Grand Theatre, drawing tears from many sentimental viewers. Achievements that are often difficult for female stars who have struggled for years came effortlessly to this new star, propelling her to instant fame. No wonder she attracts special attention.

Sullavan was originally a famous actress on Broadway in New York. She had years of experience and reputation in the opera house, but only within the confines of New York. Last year, she got married due to a moment of passionate impulse to a lucky man named Henry Fonda. However, after the marriage, they realized they were incompatible and divorced after only two months. It was Sullavan who initiated the divorce.

Because of this romance, Sullavan became the focus of Hollywood film reporters and curious onlookers. As we know, American journalists are not easy to deal with. Moreover, the questions they ask are complex and often delve into private matters. It's bad to answer poorly, and bad not to answer at all. Ordinary female stars always try their best to deal with them, but when it came to Sullavan, she was a "beautiful as peach blossoms, cold as ice" type of woman. She simply felt unable to cope. She then used the "thirty-six stratagems, running is the best" method and fled from Hollywood to New York. Her strong personality broke all Hollywood records.

When she finished filming "Only Yesterday," she suddenly disappeared. Universal searched for her everywhere, wanting to discuss her next film with her, only to find out later that she had fled back to New York. The reason was to escape the encirclement of the interviewers. However, as soon as the news spread, many people followed her to New York, and interviewers in New York swarmed around her like ants attracted to something smelly. This forced her to move to a secret location to live. But due to contractual obligations, she soon returned to Universal. She started filming her second new film, "Little Man, What Now."

Not long after the new film began shooting, she disappeared again. She went to the Hollywood airfield alone, without even a suitcase, and flew to Chicago.

But twenty-four hours later, she flew back. She said, "I was truly driven mad by these many interviewers. I had to fly to Chicago to cool down my anger."

When she returned to the set, the company staff told her, "Tomorrow is the 67th birthday of the company's president, Carl Laemmle. The company has assigned you to cut the birthday cake."

"I absolutely do not want to do that," Sullavan said bluntly. She still didn't understand Hollywood customs. Originally, this was an honorary task, because she was considered the number one female star in the company. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "The Girl from Tenth Avenue"

— Luo Ping

I Believe in You 丨 Da Shanghai

If you go to see "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" with high expectations, you may be disappointed, because not only is there no exposé, but it is also a malicious distortion of reality. Clearly, "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" presents the masses' writers from the perspective of American gentlemen.

The so-called labor movement revolutionaries, mass poets, mass painters, and mass dancers are maliciously regarded in "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" as alcoholics, sexual deviants, and unscrupulous people who make a living by deception and exaggeration. What we see on the screen are a bunch of drunkards, gamblers, thieves, lacking integrity, and without true friendship or love. What does this explain?

First of all, American gentlemen no longer dare to close their eyes and not see the expanding influence of their enemies among their masses丨丨referring to the general middle class丨丨, so they need to create some rumors and take some fictional

"facts" to confuse the public's vision.

Secondly, among the mass liberation movement activists, some people are currently living romantic private lives, allowing gentlemen to seize upon and exaggerate these points to carry out slanderous conspiracies. However, we know that no matter how austere Gandhi's personal life was, he was always an agent of British imperialism, and the romantic nature of mass liberation movement activists from the petty bourgeoisie is unavoidable. Only through practical tempering can they discard it. Moreover, a person's life is multifaceted. The fact that they strenuously engage in the mass liberation movement to advance history is naturally a cause of great distress to the gentlemen. Therefore, the gentlemen's deliberate exaggeration of the romantic side is a shameless act, isn't it easy to understand?

In any case, we should admit that "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" has completed its mission very skillfully. "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" is actually writing a love story, but it can shed the clichés of all Hollywood love stories丨丨that cheap happy-ending.

American gentlemen see that in their path of decline, many intellectuals are wavering and moving towards the historically progressive class, such as the female protagonist Marie in "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" (although it cannot explain in detail why she is wavering, it at least tells us that Marie is an intellectual with a strong sense of justice). They become afraid, so, through the mouth of a wealthy court critic, Michael, they use all kinds of unfounded provocative fictions to incite her weak soul: not only that, the theme expressed in "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" is that mass liberation movement activists are unreliable bad guys, and trustworthy are the gentlemen's court critics. And most cleverly, "The Girl from Tenth Avenue" actually allows Marie to become a "female writer" and "struggle" "alone"!

What is "struggle alone"? It is to separate the middle class from the leadership of the historically progressive class. If a grand reunion were to occur according to the general convention of American-style love stories, the audience would easily forget it immediately as a general convention, but now, there is clearly a question placed before the audience: Where exactly did Marie go? Isn't it? The kind of hazy fog symbolizing the future seen on the screen, Rosemary Ames squeezing alone in the crowd following the camera, and the sheep-like expression revealed on the face of this new star, emphatically raise this question in front of the audience, and in fact, pull the female writer into the gentlemen's camp!

As a result, the audience sympathizes with Marie, detests Keith and his companions, and admires Michael. This is the gentlemen's entire conspiracy!

The acting of Rosemary Ames and John Boles, especially the former, is successful.

RKO's New Star: Francis Lederer

— Lei

Francis Lederer, Hollywood's brand new star, recently starred in RKO's "Confessions of a Nazi Spy," appearing on the screen and meeting the world.

Lederer was born into poverty. His father was a mediocre leather merchant. He was determined to study diligently from a young age, and was very intelligent. He was particularly interested in sports and drama. When he graduated from the Prague Academy of Dramatic Arts, he received the highest honors and earned the reputation of a top student. Afterwards, he studied the structure and composition of scripts from an old actor, working tirelessly, and finally put his acting career into practice, traveling to major cities such as Berlin, Vienna, and Breslau. Because he was good at performing famous plays by Shaw, Ibsen, and Shakespeare, his reputation rose. He even co-starred with the famous actress Gitta Alpar in the play "Romeo and Juliet," which shook Europe. British people remotely expressed their admiration and hired him to perform at the Royal Theatre.

Initially, Lederer did not know English, so he hired someone to teach him. After several weeks, he memorized the dialogue of the characters and the lyrics of the songs, concentrating on memorizing them. As a result, he produced many pure English operas, which caused a sensation in the British Isles. They were performed continuously for eleven months. It can be seen that his magic is truly astonishing!

At that time, RKO's representative in the UK, Mr. Deng, met Lederer in the UK and fell in love with him at first sight. He firmly invited Lederer to perform in New York. Thus, this European theatrical giant crossed the Atlantic and contributed his life's masterpiece to the Broadway stage. His plays were performed in New York for another eight months, and he became a world-renowned actor.

Recently, he changed his goals. He gave up his stage life and jumped into the silver screen of Hollywood, striving hard. In RKO's "Confessions of a Nazi Spy," his brilliance was initially revealed, which was enough to surprise and praise people! Truly, he is not only a world-renowned stage actor, but also a big star on the silver screen.

This performance has been prepared for two months, and all rehearsals are now well-rehearsed. Film Novel

Till the Seas Run Dry and the Rocks Decay (Registered Nurse) (Part 4)

— Jie Hua

Punden packed up some tools and went to the operating room. Hatway was very happy to see her coming and asked her in a loud voice, "Is your mind stable? Good! I'm going to saw open her skull first 丨丨there's clotted blood blocking the blood vessels inside 丨丨She's gone crazy 丨丨It's been very bad for the past day or two." He explained the symptoms of the disease honestly, feeling that Punden would definitely understand. Unexpectedly, Punden's hand loosened, and the tools fell with a clang on the tiled floor. Hatway looked up and was startled to see Punden with her mouth wide open. At this moment, Shules was standing behind Punden and quickly stepped forward to support Punden. Punden wiped her forehead with her hand. Hatway looked at her with both shock and pity, and quickly said, "You're too tired. Go home and rest." Punden thanked him weakly and retreated from the operating room. Shules thought that this matter was a bit strange, Punden dropping the tools on the ground and walking away at a critical moment 丨丨 was a rare occurrence. She said to Hatway, "She just heard you say that the patient was crazy, and she was so scared." Hatway pondered. He remembered that there was also one time before when she helped him treat a mentally ill person. She also suffered the same stimulation. This is really the strangest thing. Punden in the hospital, still busy going back and forth, and Frank and his brother competed to greet her, making her even busier. There was also a young mother who was about to give birth, with a dying child next to her. Whenever Punden had some free time, she would go to see the mother and child. At this time, Hatway's surgery was successful, and the woman had regained consciousness 丨丨 which made the painful traces on Punden's face fade a lot. But Kangnaolai found her again. She was preparing a vegetarian meal for a patient in the cooking room. "Pun, what's going on? Don't you ever want to be happy?" He lowered his head to her, his sincere eyes searching her face. "Let's go out and play, we can have a very happy time, you and I!" After he finished speaking, he first took her slender hand and patted it on his face. Punden smiled softly, and completely relaxed all her defenses. When Kangnaolai reached out to hug her slender waist, she just stared at him blankly, without refusing. After a while, he hugged her tightly and whispered in her ear, "Pun, you are so lovely, I'm crazy about you!" Hearing his words, Punden unconsciously raised her hand and stroked his head. At this time, their faces were close, and their lips were getting closer and closer. Suddenly, Kangnaolai's arm hugged Punden tightly, and his lips were pressed against her mouth, passionately sucking and kissing. In this moment of confusion, Punden also kissed him back. But a moment passed, and she immediately pushed him away. Kangnaolai still tried hard to argue with her, but Punden escaped as soon as she got away. She fled to the window, her trembling hands fiddling with the curtains. Kangnaolai stared blankly at her back, not daring to chase after her, but wasn't she just kissing him back? So he mustered the remaining courage and ran up 丨丨 he knew that women were all about the same, and could never escape his grasp. He walked up and gently put his hands on her shoulders, slowly turning her around. Then he fiddled with her chin with his fingers, raising her face. Then he looked at her face and softly asked her, "Pun, what's going on? Don't you like me?" (To be continued)
